    <span class="c57"><a class="c17" href="#h.2lwamvv">Serving Data</a></span><span
      class="c57">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="c2"><a class="c17"
        href="#h.2lwamvv">13</a></span>
  </p>

  <p class="c105">
    <span class="c26"><a class="c17" href="#h.idp2g5u449zu">Appendix D: Use Case for Sensor Installation</a></span><span
      class="c26">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="c26"><a class="c17"
        href="#h.idp2g5u449zu">35</a></span>

  <p class="c30 c100 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <hr style="page-break-before: always; display: none" />
  <p class="c30 c100 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c47 c121">
      <h1 id="h.4i7ojhp" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c78 c57">Overview of Mata Elang</span>
      </h1>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-1 start" start="1">
    <li class="c97 c171 li-bullet-0">
      <h2 id="h.2xcytpi" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Mata Elang</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c95 c122">
    <span class="c2">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Many applications are
      beginning to face the challenges of big data, not to mention apps for
      analyzing network traffic [1].
    </span>
  </p>
  <p class="c122 c179">
    <span class="c2">Network Intrusion Detection System (NIDS) is an application that is
      time-sensitive and requires a solution to the big data. Big data
      challenges are usually using the concept of 4V (Volume, Velocity
      Variety, Value). However, in some cases, especially NIDS, it requires a
      deeper understanding of the idea to define it because the
      characteristics of NIDS data do not always meet the concept.[1].
    </span>
  </p>
  <p class="c122 c138">
    <span class="c2">Snort is a signature-based NIDS application that is commonly used. The
      architecture and mechanism cannot be said to be able to face the
      challenges of big data efficiently.
    </span>
  </p>
  <p class="c122 c186">
    <span class="c2">Mata Elang as one of the case studies implementing Snort NIDS as IDS
      uses the following architecture,
    </span>
  </p>
  <p class="c152 c50">
    <span class="c2">&#9679; In existing architecture, sensor placement must be on the same
      physical network with a defense center so that the deployment cost can
      be enormous.
    </span>
  </p>
  <p class="c50 c190">
    <span class="c2">&#9679; Data alert storage is still using a centralized database
      technology, where if the data stored is getting bigger in volume,
      scaling will be severe.
    </span>
  </p>
  <p class="c50 c152">
    <span class="c2">&#9679; Analytic and data aggregation is also carried out using a
      centralized system, so if the data grows more prominent, scaling will be
      critical. Of course, this implementation is not ready when &nbsp;facing
      the challenges of big data.
    </span>
  </p>
  <p class="c95 c122 c195">
    <span class="c2">Therefore, research is needed to prepare Snort NIDS to face the big
      data challenges.</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c30 c100 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-1" start="2">
    <li class="c97 c171 li-bullet-0">
      <h2 id="h.1ci93xb" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Mata Elang Community</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c174 c140 c122">
    <span class="c2">For ecosystems to work appropriately, communities of participants need
      to exist. These participants should be able to develop products and
      services based on platform resources (via APIs). Experts in the panel
      observed some critical considerations in developing an ecosystem
      community, which include the need, 1) to establish a fair and
      transparent intellectual property model whereby third party developers
      can fairly monetize their developments, 2) to open up the platform to a
      sufficient degree to allow and encourage innovation, 3) to &#39;create
      community&#39; in the sense of enabling the exchange of ideas and
      fostering collaboration, and, 4) to provide an open door for feedback
      from the community about the position and direction of the ecosystem in
      the market.</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c140 c122 c174">
    <span class="c2">By enabling people to invest and create new products and services on
      the platform, the ecosystem can provide a more productive set of options
      to end-users. Moreover, the faster an ecosystem develops a positive
      reputation among developers and thus more join the platform, the more
      difficult and tedious it becomes for others to replicate such a deed.
      This reflects market expectations driving network effects. As more
      developers are attracted to the ecosystem, more users are drawn to new
      products and better services offered.</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-0" start="2">
    <li class="c47 c121">
      <h1 id="h.3whwml4" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c78 c57">System Architecture</span>
      </h1>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c33">
    <span class="c2">We will develop a defense center system architecture for a cloud
      environment. The system block diagram for this concept, as shown in
      Figure 1:</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c48" id="h.2et92p0">
    <span class="c2">Figure 1. Cloud environment system concept for Snort-cloud-based IDS
      framework</span><span style="
          overflow: hidden;
          display: inline-block;
          margin: 0px 0px;
          border: 0px solid #000000;
          transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          width: 497.5px;
          height: 234.93px;
        "><img alt="" src="../assets/images/image9.png" style="
            width: 497.5px;
            height: 288.23px;
            margin-left: -0px;
            margin-top: -5.92px;
            transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
            -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          " title="" /></span>
  </p>
  <p class="c33">
    <span class="c2">The sensors or base modules are designed to run in the cloud computing
      environment and can be installed in the different networks from the core
      module (central defense system), as we can see in the system diagram.
      Defense centers will process and analyze reports generated by sensors.
      Figure 2 shows the recommended system architecture for the complete
      system, including the defense center, data source, and data
      serving.</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c16 c33"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <p class="c33">
    <span style="
          overflow: hidden;
          display: inline-block;
          margin: 0px 0px;
          border: 0px solid #000000;
          transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          width: 564.68px;
          height: 213.5px;
        "><img alt="" src="../assets/images/image2.png" style="
            width: 564.68px;
            height: 213.5px;
            margin-left: -0px;
            margin-top: -0px;
            transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
            -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          " title="" /></span>
  </p>
  <p class="c48">
    <span class="c2">Figure 2. System Architecture Diagram</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-1" start="3">
    <li class="c37 li-bullet-0">
      <h2 id="h.2bn6wsx" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Data Source</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c122 c187">
    <span class="c2">The first component of the data source is the IDS sensor. In this
      version of Mata Elang, the sensor use Snort&trade; as the core IDS
      engine. Soon we plan to use various &nbsp; &nbsp;IDS engines e.g
      Suricata, Wazuh, etc. &nbsp;The output of the sensors sent to the
      defense center via some types of transmission protocol, which could
      transport data at the lowest latency as possible. A fast and efficient
      transmission protocol is also mandatory for carrying sensor
      outputs.</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-1" start="4">
    <li class="c37 li-bullet-0">
      <h2 id="h.qsh70q" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Defense Center</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c122 c83">
    <span class="c2">The Defense Center is the part of the Mata Elang, the processing of
      which is maximized is the processing of data, from collecting data to
      storing data in a database. The central defense system is divided into
      three parts, namely collecting data, processing data, and storing
      data.</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-2 start" start="1">
    <li class="c139 li-bullet-1">
      <h3 id="h.1pxezwc" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c119 c134">Collecting Data</span>
      </h3>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c50 c148">
    <span class="c2">The data collection process is a continuation stage after the sensor
      receives data attacks that occur on a network. In conducting data
      collection, the system uses Apache Kafka. Kafka here is a bridge between
      the sensor and spark as the primary data processors. In the process of
      Kafka, the data will be received and processed by the MQTT server. In
      MQTT the data will be processed by coding and simplification using Kafka
      Avro. Then it will be connected to the confluent so that the data is
      ready to proceed to spark via Apache Kafka.</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-2" start="2">
    <li class="c139 li-bullet-2">
      <h3 id="h.49x2ik5" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c119 c134">Processing Data</span>
      </h3>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c50 c83">
    <span class="c2">Data processing in the Mata Elang system uses Apache Spark. The Apache
      Spark feature used in data processing is a streaming feature that can
      record and process data in live time. In streaming processing, a Spark
      will stream brokers to Kafka. The streaming process includes the
      following steps:</span>
  </p>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_12-0 start">
    <li class="c66 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">It deserializes AVRO data with an existing registry scheme.</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c66 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">It converts data into data frames for Apache Spark&#39;s data
        abstraction using the map function.</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c43 c66 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">It executes the existing data frame aggregation process using the
        subtraction function.</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c66 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">It writes to Apache Cassandra.</span>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-2 start" start="1">
    <li class="c139 li-bullet-1">
      <h3 id="h.2p2csry" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c119 c134">Storing Data</span>
      </h3>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c50 c83 c198" id="h.147n2zr">
    <span class="c2">The first part of the defense center receiving data streams from remote
      sensors and then split these data into two types of flow process: stream
      job and batch job. The stream job process serves real-time monitoring
      information, while the batch job process is used for analytical data.
    </span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-2" start="2">
    <li class="c139 li-bullet-2">
      <h3 style="display: inline">
        <span class="c119 c134">Serving Data</span>
      </h3>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c83 c161">
    <span class="c2">There are two components in the serving data module: dashboards and the
      map.</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_24-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c30 c54 c43 li-bullet-4"><span class="c2">Dashboard</span></li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c54 c83">
    <span class="c2">For the dashboards, we refer to the popular standard metrics for
      network security applications by the SANS Institute. It consists of
      :</span>
  </p>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_28-0 start">
    <li class="c75 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">Event Monitoring. It based on the result of streaming jobs</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c75 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">Event Statistics. It based on the result of streaming jobs</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c75 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">Top Signatures. It based on the result of batch jobs (the total
        number of &nbsp;event grouped by the signature&#39;s name)</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c43 c75 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">Top Protocol. It based on the result of batch jobs (the total number
        of &nbsp;event grouped by the protocol)</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c75 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">Sensor Statistics. It based on the result of batch jobs (the total
        number of the event for each sensor)</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c75 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c2">Daily-monthly-annual report</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c75 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">User-role-profile-menu-management </span>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_24-0" start="2">
    <li class="c30 c54 c43 li-bullet-4"><span class="c2">Maps</span></li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c54 c83">
    <span class="c2">A cyber threat map, also known as a cyber attack map, is a real-time
      map of the computer security attacks that are going on at any given
      time. Beams of light, represented by different colors showing where an
      attack comes from and where it is going</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-0" start="3">
    <li class="c47 c121">
      <h1 style="display: inline">
        <span class="c78 c57">System Configuration</span>
      </h1>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-1 start" start="1">
    <li class="c37 li-bullet-0">
      <h2 id="h.eysnx4dpwebu" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Minimum configuration</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c25">
    <span class="c2">The minimum configuration is a configuration with one sensor and one
      host of defense center.
    </span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-2" start="3">
    <li class="c139 li-bullet-1">
      <h3 id="h.2grqrue" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c119 c134">System configuration</span>
      </h3>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c140 c95 c184">
    <span style="
          overflow: hidden;
          display: inline-block;
          margin: 0px 0px;
          border: 0px solid #000000;
          transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          width: 565px;
          height: 213.99px;
        "><img alt="" src="../assets/images/image13.png" style="
            width: 565px;
            height: 213.99px;
            margin-left: -0px;
            margin-top: -0px;
            transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
            -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          " title="" /></span>
  </p>
  <p class="c48">
    <span class="c2">Figure 3. System Architecture Diagram</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c30 c50 c83">
    <span class="c2">Figure 3 shows the minimum configuration for Mata Elang with one sensor
      and one monitored network.</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-2" start="4">
    <li class="c139 li-bullet-2">
      <h3 id="h.er8kqxpzkk9c" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c119 c134">Network configuration</span>
      </h3>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c48">
    <span class="c2">Figure 4. Network Topology</span><span style="
          overflow: hidden;
          display: inline-block;
          margin: 0px 0px;
          border: 0px solid #000000;
          transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          width: 565px;
          height: 237.06px;
        "><img alt="" src="../assets/images/image4.png" style="
            width: 565px;
            height: 237.06px;
            margin-left: -0px;
            margin-top: -0px;
            transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
            -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          " title="" /></span>
  </p>
  <p class="c30 c50 c83">
    <span class="c2">Figure 4 shows the common topology with two switches and one PC for the
      defense center. At a minimum use of the configuration, we only use one
      sensor to monitor the private network. In this case, the sensor is
      placed in a different network address with the defense center.</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c30 c16 c95"><span class="c2"></span></p>

  </p>
  <p class="c30 c50 c83" id="h.20stsxpug9pj">
    <span class="c2">Figure 5 shows the basic system configuration where the Mata Elang can
      monitor more than one network.
    </span>
  </p>

    <span style="

  <p class="c48"><span class="c2">Figure 6. Network Topology</span></p>
  <p class="c30 c50 c83">
    <span class="c2">Figure 6 shows the physical network configuration of the Mata Elang for
      multi-sensors &nbsp; containing: &nbsp;two tappers, two sensors, two
      switches, and one defense center</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-0" start="4">
    <li class="c47 c121">
      <h1 id="h.19c6y18" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c78 c57">Version Control of Source Code </span>
      </h1>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c60">
    <span>We use &nbsp; GitHub as out application version control. Mata Elang
      Project is hosted on Github as a public organization for collaboration.
      (</span><span class="c72"><a class="c17"
        href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://github.com/mata-elang-pens&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153648879000&amp;usg=AOvVaw1rkd9zaYjbieaVk1ZgPiLn">https://github.com/mata-elang-pens</a></span><span
      class="c2">)</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c99">
    <span style="
          overflow: hidden;
          display: inline-block;
          margin: 0px 0px;
          border: 0px solid #000000;
          transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          width: 549.5px;
          height: 345.95px;
        "><img alt="" src="../assets/images/image10.png" style="
            width: 549.5px;
            height: 345.95px;
            margin-left: -0px;
            margin-top: -0px;
            transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
            -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          " title="" /></span>
  </p>
  <p class="c48" id="h.tyjcwt">
    <span class="c2">Figure 7. Mata Elang Repositories</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c30 c60">
    <span>The repository of Mata Elang is publicly accessible. Everyone can
      propose changes by forking the repository by using the pull request
      feature. Some sections in Mata Elang Architecture requires additional
      authorization by Mata Elang Founders to change as described in the </span><span class="c53">Strategic Document
      section 5.</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-1" start="3">
    <li class="c37 li-bullet-0">
      <h2 id="h.3tbugp1" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Mata Elang LTS (Long Term Support) Version 1.0</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c25">
    <span class="c2">At present, Mata Elang is in version 1.0. It means we do not rule out
      the possibility that Mata Elang will make updates in various aspects.
      So, we will do Long Term Support with the conditions below:</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-2" start="6">
    <li class="c139 li-bullet-2">
      <h3 id="h.28h4qwu" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c119 c134">Data Source</span>
      </h3>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c50 c83">
    <span class="c2">For the Long Term Support version, we do support according to the
      available versions of each requirement. Here is the Long Term Support
      Version for Data Source:</span>
  </p>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_6-0 start">
    <li class="c97 c54 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c2">Linux Ubuntu Server version 18.04 </span>
    </li>
    <li class="c97 c54 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c2">Python version 3.8.2 </span>
    </li>
    <li class="c97 c54 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">Java version 8 </span>
    </li>
    <li class="c97 c54 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c2">Python-PIP version 3.8.2 </span>
    </li>
    <li class="c97 c54 c43 li-bullet-8">

  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-0" start="5">
    <li class="c47 c121">
      <h1 id="h.3l18frh" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c57 c78">Standard Coding</span>
      </h1>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c30 c132">
    <span class="c2">The Mata Elang source code consists of several programming and
      scripting languages. The scripting language is used for automating build
      and docker containers for sensors.</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c30 c132">
    <span class="c2">For this reason, we standardized coding scheme for extensible
      development reasons:</span>
  </p>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_32-0 start">
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c2">No more than a single statement per line, for bash scripting, there
        might be a pipelining (||) or chaining (&amp;&amp;), so it is
        separated by a backslash and the new line between statements.</span><span style="
            overflow: hidden;
            display: inline-block;
            margin: 0px 0px;
            border: 0px solid #000000;
            transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
            -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
            width: 602px;
            height: 68.5px;
          "><img alt="" src="../assets/images/image1.png" style="
              width: 602px;
              height: 68.5px;
              margin-left: 0px;
              margin-top: 0px;
              transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
              -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
            " title="" /></span>
    </li>
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c2">Comments must be added for understandable reasons in every statement
        context.</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">Use of the information before including the coding script</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">Naming variables are adjusted globally for easy understand by others
      </span>
    </li>
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">Error handling will be explained in the troubleshooting section in
        Appendix C</span>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p class="c30 c16 c100"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_1-0" start="6">

  <h1 class="c81 c176" id="h.4bvk7pj"><span class="c78 c57"></span></h1>
  <h1 class="c81" id="h.wbqatkmb2nij">
    <span class="c78 c57">Appendix A: Installation manual</span>
  </h1>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_11-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c116 c71 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <h2 id="h.bcdkvvyvpnx0" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Install Data Source ( Sensor )</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_19-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c97 c43 c120 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Installing Docker </span><span class="c98"><a class="c17"
          href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://docs.docker.com/install/&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153648966000&amp;usg=AOvVaw3XIQB6SFWp1xCRMMtH5v1e">https://docs.docker.com/install/</a></span>
    </li>
    <li class="c97 c44 c43 c120 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19">Enable Docker Service</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.9c8ed8a4ef187c6b8dc86cc3e6dfde74275a3e12"></a><a id="t.7"></a>
  <table class="c9">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c103" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo systemctl enable docker</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo systemctl start docker</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_19-0" start="3">
    <li class="c32 c43 c120 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19 c44">Server preparation, configure the network interface to in promiscuous
        mode. Install </span><span class="c19">ifupdown</span><span class="c19 c44">&nbsp;package. Then, edit
      </span><span class="c19">/etc/network/interfaces</span><span class="c19 c44">&nbsp;file, add some line like the
        down below:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.cb364138a8368af4c6ad164ae33b3b464ad1235f"></a><a id="t.8"></a>
  <table class="c9">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c103" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c19 c20">auto eth1</span></p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">iface eth1 inet manual</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; &nbsp;up ip address add 0/0 dev eth1</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; &nbsp;up ip link set eth1 up</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; &nbsp;up ip link set eth1 promisc on</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; &nbsp;down ip link set eth1 promisc off</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; &nbsp;down ip link set eth1 down</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24 c16"><span class="c20 c19"></span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">auto eth2</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">iface eth2 inet dhcp</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c24 c140 c44 c16 c151"><span class="c19 c91 c107 c123"></span></p>
  <p class="c30 c151"><span class="c2">Note: </span></p>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_17-0 start">
    <li class="c97 c45 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span>Don&#39;t forget to change the </span><span class="c53">eth1</span><span>&nbsp;and </span><span
        class="c53">eth2</span><span class="c2">&nbsp;with your server network interface name</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c97 c45 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c53">eth1</span><span>&nbsp;must be connected to the tapper port where the port is set for
        mirroring destination port</span>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_19-0" start="4">
    <li class="c32 c43 c120 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19 c44">Restart network service or restart your server</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.83cdf9bfee19a8dd392e2e85587be77a8176908a"></a><a id="t.9"></a>
  <table class="c9">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c103" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo systemctl restart networking</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_19-0" start="5">
    <li class="c97 c44 c43 c120 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19 c44">Download Sensor Installer from </span><span class="c44"><a class="c17"
          href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://github.com/mata-elang-pens/sensor-installer&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153648973000&amp;usg=AOvVaw0wqsyXPbbQjjwQf4J2BjPc">mata-elang-pens/sensor-installer</a></span><span
        class="c19 c44">&nbsp;GitHub repository
        (https://github.com/mata-elang-pens/sensor-installer)</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c32 c43 c120 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19">Add executable permission to setup.sh</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.1d6665f5364be4aa42ed9e8767c456fee5e49ee6"></a><a id="t.10"></a>
  <table class="c9">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c103" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo chmod +x setup.sh</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo chmod +x update-rule.sh</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_19-0" start="7">
    <li class="c97 c44 c43 c120 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Run the setup.sh script with the following command and wait until the
        setup finished</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.79627e8901a77e039199bb0736bc4e13daf1dd86"></a><a id="t.11"></a>
  <table class="c9">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c103" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ sudo ./setup.sh</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c44 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_19-0" start="8">
    <li class="c32 c43 c120 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c19">To Update Snort Rules use this command :</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.01f5169cc2246c5c18dffe862c2f4f4e7eebd90e"></a><a id="t.12"></a>
  <table class="c9">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c103" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo ./update-rule.sh</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c32 c16"><span class="c119 c19 c91 c107"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_11-0" start="2">
    <li class="c116 c71 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <h2 id="h.mjkhxabu0fom" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Install Mosquitto</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_2-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c30 c50 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Update APT index and install the new Ubuntu Package Update</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.2a4b296e6cc1cad84b01527817878b9e7adf5876"></a><a id="t.13"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt update</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt upgrade</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c71 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_2-0" start="2">
    <li class="c30 c50 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Install mosquitto using APT</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.1e86e72f9bfa612822e92668f3f7fd61b92ef22c"></a><a id="t.14"></a>
  <table class="c137 c142">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">$ sudo apt install mosquitto mosquitto-clients</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c71 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_2-0" start="3">
    <li class="c30 c50 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c3 c44">Enable mosquitto service</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.828b4fcc8fb8f4b12ffd2abc37d92cc74fab1c83"></a><a id="t.15"></a>
  <table class="c137 c189">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c194" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">$ sudo systemctl enable mosquitto.service</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c71 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_2-0" start="4">
    <li class="c30 c50 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c3 c44">Start mosquitto service</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.90e000d123d2c4d0d5d1198037f60f27212bfe07"></a><a id="t.16"></a>
  <table class="c137 c142">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">$ sudo systemctl start mosquitto.service</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_11-0" start="3">
    <li class="c116 c71 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <h2 id="h.hn38e7k723ho" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Install Apache Cassandra</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19 c44">Add Cassandra Debian Repository</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.97874c941ca7103e48c305cc13997faeacc3718e"></a><a id="t.17"></a>
  <table class="c69">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c194" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">$ echo &ldquo;deb </span><span class="c35 c72"><a class="c17"
                href="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://www.apache.org/dist/cassandra/debian&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153648982000&amp;usg=AOvVaw1M4l4LghZFCPpJuslK7RFs">http://www.apache.org/dist/cassandra/debian</a></span><span
              class="c35 c19">&nbsp;36x main&rdquo; | sudo tee -a
              /etc/apt/sources.list.d/cassandra.list</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c45 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="2">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c3 c44">Import the Cassandra Repository key</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.a91b0d77c856c4805af1354393f3028158e91704"></a><a id="t.18"></a>
  <table class="c137 c92">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c149" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">$ curl https://downloads.apache.org/cassandra/KEYS | sudo
              apt-key add -</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c45 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="3">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c3 c44">Update the APT index</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.27a01b1471baa6c6ec87035c7b45bb3f629f3a40"></a><a id="t.19"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt update</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c45 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="4">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19 c44">If there&#39;s an error &quot;GPG error: </span><span class="c44 c98"><a class="c17"
          href="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://www.apache.org/&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153648985000&amp;usg=AOvVaw1f-hV-I3UxW9JwEZ38hsxL">http://www.apache.org</a></span><span
        class="c3 c44">&nbsp;36x InRelease: The following signatures couldn&#39;t be
        verified because the public key is not available: NO_PUBKEY
        A278B781FE4B2BDA&quot;</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.74a54caacb0e7d529647398fedb304aeb395d32f"></a><a id="t.20"></a>
  <table class="c92 c137">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c149" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt-key adv --keyserver pool.sks-keyservers.net
              --recv-key A278B781FE4B2BDA</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt update</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="5">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c3 c44">Install Cassandra using APT</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.98940778446017f551d5d6913f80d62480ea17f5"></a><a id="t.21"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt install cassandra</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="6">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c3 c44">Enable Cassandra Service</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.9a12bc9250dec59b85a033dad8752bf82e497f7c"></a><a id="t.22"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo systemctl enable cassandra.service</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="7">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c3 c44">Start Cassandra Service</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.eed98ba425de82651cadea44a04c8a108d6fdeaf"></a><a id="t.23"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo systemctl start cassandra.service</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="8">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Configuring Apache Cassandra, edit /etc/cassandra/cassandra.yaml
        file, change the authenticator, rpc_address, and broadcast_rpc_address
        like the following value below:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.eaa396b1ec15232ec9d43431f351454b136ff2d7"></a><a id="t.24"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">authenticator: PasswordAuthenticator</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">...</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">rpc_address: 0.0.0.0</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">...</span></p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">broadcast_rpc_address: localhost</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="9">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Restart Cassandra Service</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.02738487425410abf2a48b5830f2af6bafd142c6"></a><a id="t.25"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo systemctl restart cassandra.service</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="10">
    <li class="c30 c92 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c3 c44">Login to cassandra with default user</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.08cbde6a5dbcc3b2cffa4de35a0c5e31e7c07ff8"></a><a id="t.26"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ cqlsh -u cassandra -p cassandra</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16 c40"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <p class="c30 c40">
    <span class="c19 c44">NB : When there is an error </span><span class="c19 c53 c44">&quot;</span><span
      class="c19 c53 c44 c192">Connection error: (&#39;Unable to connect to any servers&#39;,
      {&#39;127.0.0.1&#39;: TypeError (&#39;ref () does not take keyword
      arguments&#39;,)})</span><span class="c19 c53 c44">&quot;</span><span class="c3 c44">. Run the command below to
      resolve this problem. After that, run the
      cqlsh command again.</span>
  </p>
  <a id="t.c045d49340ae4326abd034843dc5a3e68f1059a7"></a><a id="t.27"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt install python-pip</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ pip install cassandra-driver</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ export CQLSH_NO_BUNDLED=true</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="11">
    <li class="c30 c43 c92 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Create a new Apache Cassandra user with the following command:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.4987e3b09e68906c8be6cdfbe80d7f049ac63234"></a><a id="t.28"></a>

    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">&gt; CREATE USER </span><span class="c4">yourusername</span><span
              class="c35 c19">&nbsp;WITH PASSWORD &#39;</span><span class="c4">yourpassword</span><span
              class="c20 c19">&#39; SUPERUSER;</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_15-0" start="12">

      <span class="c3 c44">Import Apache Cassandra keyspace, copy file cassandraQueryScript.cql
        to defense center server</span>

              cassandraQueryScript.cql</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>

          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">&gt; INSERT INTO kaspa.user (username, company, email,
              first_name, group, last_name, password_hash, time_joined) VALUES
              (</span><span class="c35">&lsquo;</span><span class="c4">yourusername</span><span
              class="c35">&rsquo;</span><span class="c35 c19">, </span><span class="c35">&lsquo;</span><span
              class="c4">yourcompany</span><span class="c35">&rsquo;</span><span class="c35 c19">, &lsquo;</span><span
              class="c4">youremail@example.com</span><span class="c35 c19">&rsquo;, &lsquo;</span><span
              class="c4">yourfirstname</span><span class="c35 c19">&rsquo;, &lsquo;</span><span
              class="c4">yourgroup</span><span class="c35 c19">&rsquo;, &lsquo;</span><span
              class="c4">yourlastname</span><span class="c20 c19">&rsquo;,
              &lsquo;$6$rounds=656000$aS2RFKm/fkVcHWi1$QaltqzL92qlShWP9hG2vWIHZ1qCzRnIXApavcCBvaewGQGZArBNvQRazfMabJonZaXzmwMwuodGFYAV3h5Pzw0&rsquo;,
              toTimeStamp(now()));</span>
          </p>
        </td>

    <li class="c116 c71 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <h2 id="h.yb3ld04l31kw" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Install MongoDB</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19 c44">Import MongoDB Repository Key</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.c89bd7196c3cf4de9b7c4fa31805106729ca487c"></a><a id="t.33"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ wget -qO - https://www.mongodb.org/static/pgp/server-4.2.asc
              | sudo apt-key add -</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0" start="2">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Add MongoDB Ubuntu Repository</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.b29cd20895c0742d254c01d8cdb4f4052af43fb7"></a><a id="t.34"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">$ echo </span><span class="c19 c150">&ldquo;</span><span class="c20 c19">deb
              https://repo.mongodb.org/apt/ubuntu bionic/mongodb-org/4.2
              multiverse&rdquo; | sudo tee -a
              /etc/apt/sources.list.d/mongodb-org-4.2.list</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0" start="3">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c3 c44">Update APT index</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.27a01b1471baa6c6ec87035c7b45bb3f629f3a40"></a><a id="t.35"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>

          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt update</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0" start="4">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Install MongoDB</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.f004acaa45dce378a1820654230391eb10df05ab"></a><a id="t.36"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt install mongodb-org</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0" start="5">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Edit /etc/mongod.conf to configure IP binding and replica set in
        order to enable access to the database from outside network and enable
        change stream which is essential for real-time application (such as
        STEVIA).
      </span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.0f44676394ebdb69a76495ce6e0dc5f090a17e20"></a><a id="t.37"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">net:</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; port: 27017</span></p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; bindIp: 0.0.0.0</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">... </span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">replication:</span></p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; replSetName: rs0</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0" start="6">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Enable Mongo Service</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.95231a1a260a1e919e60f82972dee7dcec80ab7e"></a><a id="t.38"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo systemctl enable mongod.service</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0" start="7">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Start Mongo Service</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.738cc97ec5ee889ebc64d6b19514bb0f4c9561c9"></a><a id="t.39"></a>
  <table class="c39">

      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">

        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0" start="8">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c3 c44">Create an admin user for MongoDB and initiate the replica set using
        the following command inside mongo-shell:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.22c93f43765d76a2ea55c779f438d404ecbd5b1b"></a><a id="t.40"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ mongo</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">&gt; use admin</span></p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">&gt; db.createUser({user: &ldquo;</span><span class="c4">yourusername</span><span
              class="c35 c19">&rdquo;, pwd: &ldquo;</span><span class="c4">yourpassword</span><span
              class="c20 c19">&rdquo;, roles: [&ldquo;root&rdquo;]})</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">&gt; db.getUsers()</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">&gt; rs.initiate()</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_29-0" start="9">
    <li class="c0 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c3 c44">Edit /etc/mongod.conf file again to enable the authentication, change
        the following section like below:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.0a1fc313f3ae4a4b9959b787577b14d301923e5f"></a><a id="t.41"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">...</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">security:</span></p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">&nbsp; authorization: &#39;enabled&#39;</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">...</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c0">
    <span class="c3 c44">Note: admin user must be created while the authorization is
      disabled</span>
  </p>

    <li class="c71 c43 c116 li-bullet-3">
      <h2 id="h.lk8brjnfjaqq" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Install Apache Hadoop ( Single Node Cluster Installation )</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_22-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c31 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c3 c44">The required additional step before the Hadoop installation :</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_16-0 start">
    <li class="c63 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Java installation (minimum version 8) OpenJDK/Oracle</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c43 c63 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c3 c44">Set the JAVA_HOME environment variable</span>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_22-0" start="2">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19 c44">Download Hadoop</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.42f71b1594c0f12361d9cf3de303579158773204"></a><a id="t.43"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ wget
              https://www-eu.apache.org/dist/hadoop/common/hadoop-3.2.1/hadoop-3.2.1.tar.gz</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_22-0" start="3">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c3 c44">Extract the Hadoop archive</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.95226bd56f811bfa69caae3840c2f63441a892b5"></a><a id="t.44"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ tar -xzf hadoop-3.2.1.tar.gz</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_22-0" start="4">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Rename the hadoop directory name</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.2927859000e6a93994989a3d17a172d1330002b2"></a><a id="t.45"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ mv hadoop-3.2.1 hadoop</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16 c40"><span class="c119 c19 c91 c107"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_22-0" start="5">
    <li class="c32 c43 c40 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c3 c44">(optional) Remove the downloaded archive to save space</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.9f30cd0f882d204ae496528391317d8e4ac5ec38"></a><a id="t.46"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ rm -f hadoop-3.2.1.tar.gz</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_22-0" start="6">
    <li class="c32 c43 c40 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19 c44">Add Hadoop to user PATH, edit /home/yourusername/.bashrc with any
        text editor (ex: </span><span class="c19 c44 c107">nano .bashrc</span><span class="c3 c44">), add this line at
        the bottom:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.87044316a2411a9c5ee61bd4433e6453c6291c48"></a><a id="t.47"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">HADOOP_HOME=/home/</span><span class="c4">yourusername</span><span
              class="c20 c19">/hadoop</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">PATH=$PATH:$HADOOP_HOME/bin:$HADOOP_HOME/sbin</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c3 c44"></span></p>

  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_22-0" start="9">
    <li class="c32 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c3 c44">Make sure you can connect using ssh to the localhost without a
        password. If ssh still asks the password run these command and then
        check again:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.25c15cd0a639e96fd7630ecb739f30d925666584"></a><a id="t.50"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ ssh-keygen -t rsa -P &#39;&#39; -f ~/.ssh/id_rsa</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub &gt;&gt; ~/.ssh/authorized_keys</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ chmod 0600 ~/.ssh/authorized_keys</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>

          </p>

      <span class="c19">Make sure you already installed Docker at the Defense Center
        environment, see </span><span><a class="c17"
          href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://docs.docker.com/install/&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153649029000&amp;usg=AOvVaw2XGWi1DhceTCfPCJbPFq-r">https://docs.docker.com/install/</a></span><span
        class="c19">&nbsp;for Docker installation tutorial.</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c32 c43 c40 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19 c44">Edit </span><span class="c19">docker-compose.yml</span><span class="c19 c44">&nbsp;file,
        find the line contain this :</span>
    </li>

        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">

              PLAINTEXT://broker:29092,PLAINTEXT_HOST://</span><span class="c1">yourip</span><span
              class="c35 c19 c107 c141">:9092</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c44 c40 c94">

      your host IP</span>
