    <li class="c116 c71 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <h2 id="h.q3tzra4v0b1a" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Install Apache Spark</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c18 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19">Make sure you already installed Docker at Defense Center environment,
        see </span><span class="c98"><a class="c17"
          href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://docs.docker.com/install/&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153649036000&amp;usg=AOvVaw0sq-1eOQnQWM8vnRmJPAnm">https://docs.docker.com/install/</a></span><span
        class="c3">&nbsp;for Docker installation tutorial.</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c97 c45 c44 c16"><span class="c3"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="2">
    <li class="c18 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c19">Edit docker-compose.yml file, change &lt;your-ip&gt; with your host
        IP, and then save it.</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c97 c45 c44 c16"><span class="c3"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="3">
    <li class="c31 li-bullet-5"><span class="c19">Pull the image</span></li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.d92c9e097893d564a5ba4da5ac040c77e402f756"></a><a id="t.64"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ docker-compose pull</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="4">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Clone the KaspaCoreSystem repository, then navigate the terminal to
        that directory.</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.c2c9ae64d6e14742b1d0211f640bffdc41f3d415"></a><a id="t.65"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ git clone
              https://github.com/mata-elang-pens/KaspaCoreSystem.git
              &amp;&amp; cd KaspaCoreSystem</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c45 c16"><span class="c108 c19"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="5">
    <li class="c64 c44 c43 c40 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c19">Change the value in src/main/resources/application.conf to match your
        environment.</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c45 c44 c16 c64"><span class="c3"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="6">
    <li class="c18 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19">Also change the MongoDB IP from 127.0.0.1 to your IP in
        src/main/scala/me/mamotis/kaspacore/jobs/DataStream.scala</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c97 c45 c44 c16"><span class="c3"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="7">
    <li class="c31 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19">Run these command from KaspaCoreSystem directory:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.e74b7903a95c930869160f8df637cffb28bac49b"></a><a id="t.66"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ sbt assembly</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="8">
    <li class="c18 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19">Copy target/scala-2.11/KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar file to defense
        center and place to this directory with docker-compose.yml and other
        files.</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c97 c45 c44 c16"><span class="c3"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="9">
    <li class="c31 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Start Docker services in daemon mode using these command:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.b684b98763d4126da96477a2c316213ad2b702a9"></a><a id="t.67"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ docker-compose up -d</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="10">
    <li class="c31 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Make sure that all service running</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.d457008d93f1bb3f5ebb62a6a423bacc177548cf"></a><a id="t.68"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ docker-compose ps</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="11">
    <li class="c31 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19">Open the web browser, and navigate to http://your-server-ip:8080,
        check if there is still running app, if not, try restarting the
        spark-submit service and then check again :</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.452b308fb3c2478f2f7988ed465f9187f6f002d0"></a><a id="t.69"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ docker-compose start spark-submit</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="12">
    <li class="c31 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Next, we need to set up the scheduled batch job. First, create a
        directory to place the required files for the batch job.</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.2c01f3b29585ac99f31ded87b73eb767e36accff"></a><a id="t.70"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo mkdir -p /etc/mataelang-spark</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="13">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c19">Create a new file called spark.env</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.942e8354e5f22e9dffaacba1c1c04f17ae708dc2"></a><a id="t.71"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo nano /etc/mataelang-spark/spark.env</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c40">
    <span class="c19 c91 c107 c147"><br /></span><span class="c19">add the following lines to the spark.env file (just
      change the
      SPARK_MASTER_HOST with your server IP)</span>
  </p>
  <a id="t.e8d88cf31b81aca2cfb197799a96439cfd38b496"></a><a id="t.72"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">SPARK_MASTER_HOST: </span><span class="c20 c128">yourip</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">SPARK_MASTER_PORT: 7077</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">SPARK_TOTAL_EXECUTOR_CORES: 1</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">SPARK_CONF_FILE_PATH: /opt/spark.conf</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">SPARK_SUBMIT_JAR: file:///opt/KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c40">
    <span class="c19"><br />Next, create a new file called spark.conf</span>
  </p>
  <a id="t.d512a4349768c06770a0d42b354f4e570590c9e9"></a><a id="t.73"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo nano /etc/mataelang-spark/spark.conf</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c40">
    <span class="c19 c107"><br /></span><span class="c19">and then add the following lines to the spark.conf file</span>
  </p>
  <a id="t.e3d58b88740e694b26ea48a21b1613a5cff34261"></a><a id="t.74"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">spark.submit.deployMode=client</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">spark.executor.cores=1</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">spark.executor.memory=2g</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16 c40"><span class="c108 c19"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="14">
    <li class="c31 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19">Copy application file (KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar) to the
        /etc/mataelang-spark/</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.04722e9a9cb05e60417fe90f76882a5a7ee52251"></a><a id="t.75"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c35 c19">$ sudo cp </span><span class="c4">/path/to/</span><span
              class="c20 c19">KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar /etc/mataelang-spark/</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_25-0" start="15">
    <li class="c30 c43 c40 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Add cronjob for the KaspaCoreSystem batch job. Run the following
        command to open the crontab file:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.694d244da86efd81f5775d9d6e9903ebf2c8e5f7"></a><a id="t.76"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ sudo crontab -e</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <p class="c30 c40">
    <span class="c19">After the text editor opened, add the following line :</span>
  </p>
  <a id="t.392ca285f4b923c8d3256c21b8396c01982e7516"></a><a id="t.77"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">0 0 * * * docker run --rm --name spark-submit-daily --network
              host -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime -v
              /etc/timezone:/etc/timezone -v
              /etc/mataelang-spark/spark.conf:/opt/spark.conf -v
              /etc/mataelang-spark/KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar:/opt/KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar
              --env-file /etc/mataelang-spark/spark.env -e
              SPARK_SUBMIT_CLASS=me.mamotis.kaspacore.jobs.DailyCount
              mfscy/me-spark-submit:latest</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">0 0 1 * * docker run --rm --name spark-submit-monthly --network
              host -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime -v
              /etc/timezone:/etc/timezone -v
              /etc/mataelang-spark/spark.conf:/opt/spark.conf -v
              /etc/mataelang-spark/KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar:/opt/KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar
              --env-file /etc/mataelang-spark/spark.env -e
              SPARK_SUBMIT_CLASS=me.mamotis.kaspacore.jobs.MonthlyCount
              mfscy/me-spark-submit:latest</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">0 0 1 1 * docker run --rm --name spark-submit-yearly --network
              host -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime -v
              /etc/timezone:/etc/timezone -v
              /etc/mataelang-spark/spark.conf:/opt/spark.conf -v
              /etc/mataelang-spark/KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar:/opt/KaspaCore-assembly-0.1.jar
              --env-file /etc/mataelang-spark/spark.env -e
              SPARK_SUBMIT_CLASS=me.mamotis.kaspacore.jobs.AnnuallyCount
              mfscy/me-spark-submit:latest</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c16 c96"><span class="c19 c91 c107 c119"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_11-0" start="8">
    <li class="c116 c71 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <h2 id="h.5yv1azihd0dc" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Install Dashboard</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_31-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c24 c140 c45 c44 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19">Make sure you already installed Docker at Defense Center environment,
        see </span><span class="c98"><a class="c17"
          href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://docs.docker.com/install/&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153649049000&amp;usg=AOvVaw3igU842nU3p4CzAjHvRxMu">https://docs.docker.com/install/</a></span><span
        class="c3">&nbsp;for Docker installation tutorial.</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c6 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c19">Don&#39;t forget to fill the two files kaspaclient.env and
        kaspaservice.env</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="c6">
    <span class="c19">List form in the kaspaclient.env file :</span>
  </p>
  <a id="t.9fd0e50ba6773ecf28e8a093673aa05a8e14149c"></a><a id="t.78"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">API_HOST=</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">API_USER=</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">API_PASS=</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">SECRET_TOKEN=</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">SECRET_PASSWORD=</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">SECRET_KEY=</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c24 c140 c45 c44 c16"><span class="c3"></span></p>
  <p class="c24 c45 c44 c140">
    <span class="c19">List form in the kaspaservice.env file</span>
  </p>
  <a id="t.0417ca3f8969cc9bb5f48feb8e1a3ea6e685b341"></a><a id="t.79"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">CASSANDRA_USERNAME=</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">CASSANDRA_PASSWORD=</span></p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">CASSANDRA_CLUSTER_HOST=</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">DEFAULT_OINKCODE=</span></p>
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">SECRET_KEY=</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c24 c140 c45 c44 c16"><span class="c3"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_31-0" start="3">
    <li class="c97 c45 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Pull the image</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.d92c9e097893d564a5ba4da5ac040c77e402f756"></a><a id="t.80"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ docker-compose pull</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_31-0" start="4">
    <li class="c97 c45 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c19">Start Docker services in daemon mode using these command:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.b684b98763d4126da96477a2c316213ad2b702a9"></a><a id="t.81"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ docker-compose up -d</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c45 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_31-0" start="5">
    <li class="c97 c45 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c19">Make sure that all service running</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.d457008d93f1bb3f5ebb62a6a423bacc177548cf"></a><a id="t.82"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ docker-compose ps</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c97 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_31-0" start="6">
    <li class="c56 c45 c44 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19">Open a web browser, and navigate to http://your-server-ip:8800</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_11-0" start="9">
    <li class="c116 c71 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <h2 id="h.p282qwd2zpnb" style="display: inline">
        <span class="c13">Install Stevia Visualization</span>
      </h2>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_27-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">The stevia repository clone from GitHub uses the following
        syntax:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.6aa02100788410c4e988844ac6b134fe63e18cdc"></a><a id="t.83"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ git clone https://github.com/azlkiniue/stevia.git</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c119 c57 c107"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_27-0" start="2">
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">After the cloning process is complete, then enter into the stevia
        folder, and then edit the configuration file using the following
        syntax:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.e23d9ad8c24d9c5f590cdd5a5e706a89cb66a365"></a><a id="t.84"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ nano stevia/resources/values.js</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c119 c57 c107"></span></p>
  <p class="c30 c45">
    <span class="c2">then adjust the IP address and the main location with the display to be
      visualized.</span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_27-0" start="3">
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c2">Next, to install stevia, we use the npm command, which is:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.a5b59222a2b42c2af339c447800bc76d7f7fe7da"></a><a id="t.85"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24"><span class="c20 c19">$ npm install</span></p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c119 c57 c107"></span></p>
  <p class="c30 c45">
    <span>To run stevia in the background, use the following syntax:</span>
  </p>
  <a id="t.9cace1c1cf4180cb99afa7bea7a2da9c04535eb4"></a><a id="t.86"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ nohup npm start &amp;</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c119 c57 c107"></span></p>
  <p class="c30 c45">
    <span>Or, you can use other tools, such as </span><span class="c72"><a class="c17"
        href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.npmjs.com/package/forever&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153649056000&amp;usg=AOvVaw0qQ5qcis_BW1wiJCrp2pcf">forever</a></span><span>&nbsp;and
    </span><span class="c72"><a class="c17"
        href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.npmjs.com/package/nodemon&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153649057000&amp;usg=AOvVaw06DRD9FzEbEEwEaIVpmjGN">nodemon</a></span><span
      class="c119 c57 c107">.</span>
  </p>
  <p class="c30 c45">
    <span>The application will be available at port 1228.</span>
  </p>
  <h1 class="c81" id="h.2r0uhxc">
    <span class="c78 c57">Appendix B: Low Bandwidth Installation Manual</span>
  </h1>
  <p class="c30 c133">
    <span class="c2">In installing Low Bandwidth, a new registration docker will be
      provided. so that it will be lighter to install on low bandwidth
      internet. for the installation steps will follow the installation manual
      that has been provided above.</span>
  </p>
  <h1 class="c47" id="h.1664s55">
    <span class="c78 c57">Appendix C: Troubleshooting</span>
  </h1>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_34-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c97 c71 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">When installing Apache Cassandra</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_30-0 start">
    <li class="c30 c45 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19 c44">If there&#39;s an error &quot;GPG error: </span><span class="c44 c98"><a class="c17"
          href="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://www.apache.org/&amp;sa=D&amp;source=editors&amp;ust=1613153649058000&amp;usg=AOvVaw0611tOxlalxNgYdSttiTXe">http://www.apache.org</a></span><span
        class="c19 c44">&nbsp;36x InRelease: The following signatures couldn&#39;t be
        verified because the public key is not available: NO_PUBKEY
        A278B781FE4B2BDA&quot;</span>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <a id="t.b31deb665ed0025e990ea5b6c31a7545951b7743"></a><a id="t.87"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt-key adv --keyserver pool.sks-keyservers.net
              --recv-key A278B781FE4B2BDA &amp;&amp; sudo apt update</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_34-0" start="2">
    <li class="c97 c71 c43 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">When Installing Apache Hadoop</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_3-0 start">
    <li class="c97 c45 c44 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c3 c44">If you have a Portainer installed on port 9000 change the Hadoop port
        to other than 9000 or change the Portainer port. Don&#39;t forget to
        change the KaspaCoreSystem application.conf too</span>
    </li>
    <li class="c45 c44 c43 c97 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c3 c44">If you check the version of Hadoop, and there is an error $JAVA_HOME
        not found. Check whether java is installed or not. Make sure that the
        java in use is java version 8.</span>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_34-0" start="3">
    <li class="c97 c71 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c2">When installing the Defense Center</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <ul class="c28 lst-kix_list_5-0 start">
    <li class="c97 c45 c44 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span class="c19">If Kafka connector doesn&#39;t connect, please restart the </span><span
        class="c19 c107">connect-add</span><span class="c3">&nbsp;service using these command and then try checking
        again:</span>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <a id="t.9e02fef9731e46842c6d78ab5075095f617b7d3f"></a><a id="t.88"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ docker-compose start connect-add</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c16 c32"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_34-0" start="4">
    <li class="c30 c71 c43 li-bullet-8">
      <span>When there is an error &quot;</span><span class="c53">Connection error: (&#39;Unable to connect to any
        servers&#39;,
        {&#39;127.0.0.1&#39;: TypeError (&#39;ref () does not take keyword
        arguments&#39;,)})</span><span class="c2">&quot; please use the following syntax:</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.c045d49340ae4326abd034843dc5a3e68f1059a7"></a><a id="t.89"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo apt install python-pip</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ pip install cassandra-driver</span>
          </p>
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ export CQLSH_NO_BUNDLED=true</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_34-0" start="5">
    <li class="c30 c43 c71 li-bullet-3">
      <span class="c2">When the Hadoop version didn&rsquo;t found after executing hadoop
        version command, run the following command :
      </span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.8c60e71c6ed7b563ab43bb197816a13c3646c2c1"></a><a id="t.90"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ export JAVA_HOME=/usr/lib/jvm/java-8-openjdk-amd64</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c16"><span class="c2"></span></p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_34-0" start="6">
    <li class="c30 c71 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c2">When error happened while starting Hadoop dfs because JAVA_HOME not
        set or not found, edit the hadoop.env file in $HADOOP_HOME/etc/hadoop/
        directory. And set the JAVA_HOME with the installed java directory.
        Example :
      </span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.1a2a931e47f9048e8afd781db24ee7b2a8e6aabd"></a><a id="t.91"></a>

          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <h1 class="c47" id="h.idp2g5u449zu">
    <span class="c78 c57">Appendix D: Use Case for Sensor Installation</span>
  </h1>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_8-0 start" start="1">
    <li class="c97 c71 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c2">Copy the Mata Elang sensor installation file. </span>
    </li>
    <li class="c30 c71 c43 li-bullet-5">
      <span class="c2">Make sure we are in the sensor directory, then give permission to
        setup.sh and update rule.sh with the command as shown.</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.1e12437b7845f747903d426e89b647e6353ef8d3"></a><a id="t.92"></a>
  <table class="c39">
    <tbody>
      <tr class="c5">
        <td class="c36" colspan="1" rowspan="1">
          <p class="c24">
            <span class="c20 c19">$ sudo chmod +x setup.sh update-rule.sh</span>
          </p>
        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
  <p class="c30 c71 c16"><span class="c123 c57 c162"></span></p>
  <p class="c30 c71"><span class="c2">Example : </span></p>
  <p class="c30 c71">
    <span style="
          overflow: hidden;
          display: inline-block;
          margin: 0px 0px;

          -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          width: 579px;
          height: 119px;
        "><img alt="" src="../assets/images/image11.png" style="
            width: 579px;
            height: 411.99px;
            margin-left: -0px;
            margin-top: -0px;

            -webkit-transform: rotate(0rad) translateZ(0px);
          " title="" /></span>
  </p>
  <ol class="c28 lst-kix_list_8-0" start="3">
    <li class="c30 c71 c43 li-bullet-4">
      <span class="c2">Install setup.sh, using the sudo setup.sh command. When the command
        is run, several installation questions will be presented as shown
        below.</span>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <a id="t.79627e8901a77e039199bb0736bc4e13daf1dd86"></a><a id="t.93"></a>

    <tbody>

        </td>
      </tr>
    </tbody>
  </table>
